global_monetary_reference = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		value = money_value_rapported_inflation
	}
}

money_value_reference_currency = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		value = money_value
	}
}

money_value_rapported_inflation_reference_currency = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		value = money_value_rapported_inflation
	}
}

money_supply_reference_currency = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		value = money_supply
	}
}

money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country_reference_currency = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		value = money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
	}
}

relation_with_reference_currency = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root >= 80
			}
			add = 3
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= 79
				relations:root >= 50
			}
			add = 2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= 49
				relations:root >= 20
			}
			add = 1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root >= -19
				relations:root <= 19
			}
			add = 0
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= -20
				relations:root >= -49
			}
			add = -1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= -50
				relations:root >= -80
			}
			add = -2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root < -80
			}
			add = -3
		}
	}
}

infamy_of_reference_currency = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy < 24.9
				infamy = infamy_threshold:Reputable
			}
			add = 0
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy >= 25
				#infamy < 49.9
				infamy = infamy_threshold:infamous
			}
			add = -1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy >= 50
				#infamy < 99.9
				infamy = infamy_threshold:notorious

			}
			add = -2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy > 100
				infamy = infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
			add = -3
		}
	}
}

score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = {
	add = relation_with_reference_currency
	add = infamy_of_reference_currency
}

#what is the reserve currency

#money
reference_currency_is_money = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
			has_law = law_type:law_money_currency
		}
		add = 1
	}
}

# ██║     ██║   ██║██╔██╗ ██║██║     █████╗  ██████╔╝██╔██╗ ██║██║██╔██╗ ██║██║  ███╗    ██████╔╝██║     ███████║ ╚████╔╝ █████╗  ██████╔╝
# ██║     ██║   ██║██║╚██╗██║██║     ██╔══╝  ██╔══██╗██║╚██╗██║██║██║╚██╗██║██║   ██║    ██╔═══╝ ██║     ██╔══██║  ╚██╔╝  ██╔══╝  ██╔══██╗

player_has_central_bank = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		add = 1
	}
}

money_value_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_value
	}
}

money_value_rapported_inflation_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_value_rapported_inflation
	}
}

money_supply_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_supply
	}
}

money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country_of_player = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		value = money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
	}
}

relation_with_player = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root >= 80
			}
			add = 3
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= 79
				relations:root >= 50
			}
			add = 2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= 49
				relations:root >= 20
			}
			add = 1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root >= -19
				relations:root <= 19
			}
			add = 0
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= -20
				relations:root >= -49
			}
			add = -1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root <= -50
				relations:root >= -80
			}
			add = -2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				relations:root < -80
			}
			add = -3
		}
	}
}

infamy_of_player = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy < 24.9
				infamy = infamy_threshold:Reputable
			}
			add = 0
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy >= 25
				#infamy < 49.9
				infamy = infamy_threshold:infamous
			}
			add = -1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy >= 50
				#infamy < 99.9
				infamy = infamy_threshold:notorious

			}
			add = -2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				#infamy > 100
				infamy = infamy_threshold:pariah
			}
			add = -3
		}
	}
}

score_of_trust_with_player = {
	add = relation_with_player
	add = infamy_of_player
}

#what is the currency

#money
currency_of_player_is_money = {
	value = 0
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
			has_law = law_type:law_money_currency
		}
		add = 1
	}
}

		limit = {
			is_player = yes
            stockpiling_money_state > 100000000
		}
		add = 1
	}

	multiply = money_value

	subtract = gold_reserves
}

	value = money_value_rapported_inflation
	divide = global_monetary_reference
}

#devaluation
devaluation_rate_normalized = {
	value = var:devaluation_rate
	add = 100
	divide = 100
}

money_value_predicted_devaluation = {
	value = national_capacity
	divide = money_supply_predicted_devaluation
	max = 100
}

money_supply_predicted_revaluation = {
	value = money_supply
	add = money_supply_predicted_add_revaluation_1
}

money_supply_predicted_devaluation = {
	value = money_supply
	multiply = devaluation_rate_normalized
}

money_supply_predicted_add_devaluation_1 = {
	value = money_supply_predicted_devaluation
	subtract = money_supply
}
inflation_value_predicted_devaluation = { 
	add = devaluation_rate_normalized
	subtract = 1
	divide = var:devaluation_time #pas besoin de le validé car les bouton sont intouchable
}

devaluation_time_month = {
	value = var:devaluation_time 
	multiply = 12
}

devaluation_time_1_month = { #special for exchange control
	value = var:devaluation_time_1
	multiply = 12
}

devaluation_time_week = {
	value = var:devaluation_time
	multiply = 52
} 

inflation_value_predicted_devaluation_month = {
	value = var:devaluation_rate
    divide = devaluation_time_month
}

money_supply_to_add_per_month = { #valeur à ajouter par an 
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}
		add = var:money_supply_predicted_add_devaluation_1_month_valided #valided to save the vare 
		divide = devaluation_time_month
	}
}

devaluation_on_time_scripted = {
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:devaluation_on = 1
		}
		add = devaluation_time_month
		subtract = var:devaluation_on_time
	}
}

#revaluation
revaluation_rate_normalized = {
	value = 100
	subtract = var:revaluation_rate
	divide = 100
}

money_value_predicted_revaluation = {
	value = national_capacity
	divide = money_supply_predicted_revaluation
	max = 100
}

money_supply_predicted_revaluation = {
	value = money_supply
	add = money_supply_predicted_add_revaluation_1
}

money_supply_state_predicted_revaluation = {
	value = money_supply_state #money_supply
	multiply = revaluation_rate_normalized
}
money_supply_predicted_add_revaluation_1 = { #money_supply_to_subtract_per_month
	value = money_supply_state_predicted_revaluation #money_supply
	subtract = money_supply_state
}
inflation_value_predicted_revaluation = {
	add = revaluation_rate_normalized
	subtract = 1	
	multiply = var:revaluation_time
}

revaluation_time_month = {
	value = var:revaluation_time 
	multiply = 12
}

revaluation_time_1_month = { #special for exchange control
	value = var:revaluation_time_1
	multiply = 12
}

revaluation_time_week = {
	value = var:revaluation_time
	multiply = 52
}

inflation_value_predicted_revaluation_month = {
	value = var:revaluation_rate
    divide = revaluation_time_month
	multiply = -1
}

money_supply_to_subtract_per_month = {
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:revaluation_on = 1
		}
		add = var:money_supply_predicted_add_revaluation_1_month_valided #valided to save the vare 
		divide = revaluation_time_month
	}
}

revaluation_on_time_scripted = { #valeur à ajouter par an 
	value = 0
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			var:revaluation_on = 1
		}
		add = revaluation_time_month
		subtract = var:revaluation_on_time
	}
}

# ███╗   ███╗ ██████╗ ███╗   ██╗███████╗██╗   ██╗    ██╗   ██╗ █████╗ ██╗     ██╗   ██╗███████╗       
# ████╗ ████║██╔═══██╗████╗  ██║██╔════╝╚██╗ ██╔╝    ██║   ██║██╔══██╗██║     ██║   ██║██╔════╝       
# ██╔████╔██║██║   ██║██╔██╗ ██║█████╗   ╚████╔╝     ██║   ██║███████║██║     ██║   ██║█████╗         
# ██║╚██╔╝██║██║   ██║██║╚██╗██║██╔══╝    ╚██╔╝      ╚██╗ ██╔╝██╔══██║██║     ██║   ██║██╔══╝         
# ██║ ╚═╝ ██║╚██████╔╝██║ ╚████║███████╗   ██║███████╗╚████╔╝ ██║  ██║███████╗╚██████╔╝███████╗       
# ╚═╝     ╚═╝ ╚═════╝ ╚═╝  ╚═══╝╚══════╝   ╚═╝╚══════╝ ╚═══╝  ╚═╝  ╚═╝╚══════╝ ╚═════╝ ╚══════╝

money_value_0 = {
	value = national_capacity
	divide = money_supply
	max = 100
}

money_value_no_bc = {
	value = 0.1
}

money_value = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			not = {
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
			}
		}
		value = money_value_no_bc
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
			not = {
				is_subject = yes
				is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
			}
		}
		value = money_value_0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				is_subject = yes
				is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
			}
			overlord = {
				has_modifier = has_central_bank
			}
		}
		value = overlord.money_value #overlord.money_value_0
		divide = overlord.var:parity_scaled_by_the_overlord
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			or = {
				is_subject = yes
				is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
			}
			overlord = {
				not = {
					has_modifier = has_central_bank
				}
			}
		}
		value = money_value_no_bc
		divide = overlord.var:parity_scaled_by_the_overlord
	}
	min = 0.0001
}


money_value_rapported_inflation = {
	value = money_value
	multiply = inflation_value_for_currency
	min = 0.00001
}

money_supply_state_monthly = { #ex money_supply_montly 
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				money_supply < money_value_target
				any_scope_building = {
					or = {
						has_active_production_method = pm_no_monetary_policy
						has_active_production_method = pm_revaluation_25
						has_active_production_method = pm_revaluation_50
						has_active_production_method = pm_revaluation_75
						has_active_production_method = pm_revaluation_100
					}
				}
				not  = {
					or = {
						is_subject = yes
						is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_money_currency
			}
			add = var:stockpiling_money_c_var_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_dollar_currency
			}
			add = var:stockpiling_dollar_c_var_2

money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country_indexed_prestige_to_buy = {
	value = money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
	multiply = {
		value = 1
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige < 500
			}
			multiply = 1.90 #money supply must be 1.95 sup at money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 500
				prestige < 1000

			}
			multiply = 1.80 #money supply must be 1.95 sup at money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 1000
				prestige < 1500

			}
			multiply = 1.70  #money supply must be 1.95 sup at money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 1500
				prestige < 2000

			}
			multiply = 1.60
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 2500
				prestige < 3000

			}
			multiply = 1.50
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 3000
				prestige < 3500


			}
			multiply = 1.40
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 4000
				prestige < 4500

			}
			multiply = 1.30
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 4500
				prestige < 5000

			}
			multiply = 1.20
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 5000
			}
			multiply = 1.10
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 10000
			}
			multiply = 0.90  #money supply must be 0.90 sup at money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country 25% sup more the value is smal more currency is demanded out of the frontier
		}
	}
}

money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country_indexed_prestige_to_sell = {
	value = money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
	multiply = {
		value = 1
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige < 500
			}
			multiply = 1.8
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 500
				prestige < 1000

			}
			multiply = 1.7
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 1000
				prestige < 1500

			}
			multiply = 1.6
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 1500
				prestige < 2000

			}
			multiply = 1.5
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 2000
				prestige < 2500

			}
			multiply = 1.4
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 2500
				prestige < 3000


			}
			multiply = 1.3
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 3000
				prestige < 3500

			}
			multiply = 1.2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 3500
				prestige < 4000

			}
			multiply = 1.2
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 4000
				prestige < 4500

			}
			multiply = 1.1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 4500
				prestige < 5000

			}
			multiply = 1
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 5000
			}
			multiply = 0.90
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				prestige >= 10000
			}
			multiply = 0.80  #money supply must be 0.90 sup at money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country 25% sup more the value is smal more currency is demanded out of the frontier
		}
	}
}

	multiplier = 0.90

	add = var:money_value_target_2
}

money_value_target = {
	add = national_capacity
	divide = var:money_value_target_1  #valeur à choisir
}

total_gold_reserves = {
	add = gold_reserves
}

central_bank_gold_reserves = {
	value = stockpiling_central_bank_gold_reserves_var_0
}

central_bank_gold_reserves_state = {
	value = 1
	add  = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
				}
				add = var:central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}

central_bank_gold_reserves_state_25 = {
	value = 1
	add  = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
				}
				add = var:central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
			}
		}
	}
	multiply = 0.25
}

country_credit = {
	value = credit
	multiply = -1
}

national_capacity = {
	value = 1
	if = {
		add = gold_reserves
		#add = country_credit
		add = central_bank_gold_reserves_state
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					is_player = yes
					gold_balance_scripted > 0
				}
			}
			add = gold_balance_scripted
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_technology_researched = gold_exchange_standard #remplacer par une loi à voir
			}
			add = reference_currency_owned_by_the_country_in_gold
		}
	}
	min = 0.01
}

	value = 1
	divide = prestige #country_rank
	multiply = 1000
}

vo_interest_value = {
	value = 0.01
	multiply = country_rank_scale

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_variable = bank_interest
		}
		add = var:bank_interest
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AAA
		}
		add = 0.025
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_AA
		}
		add = 0.05
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_A
		}
		add = 0.075
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BBB
		}
		add = 0.1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_BB
		}
		add = 0.15
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_B
		}
		add = 0.20
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CCC
		}
		add = 0.25
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_CC
		}
		add = 0.30
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = country_credit_rating_C
		}
		add = 0.30

#money
money_c_market_goods_buy_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:money_c.market_goods_buy_orders
	}
}
money_c_market_goods_sell_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:money_c.market_goods_sell_orders
	}
}
money_c_market_goods_delta = {
	value = money_c_market_goods_sell_orders
	subtract = money_c_market_goods_buy_orders
}
stockpiling_money_c_var_0 = {
	value = 0
	add = var:stockpiling_money_c_var_1
	add = var:circulating_money_c_var_1
}
stockpiling_money_state = {
	value = 0
	add  = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
				}
				add = var:stockpiling_money_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}
money_c_global_stokpile = {
	value = {
        add = {
            every_country = {
				add = stockpiling_money_state
            }
        }
	}
}

money_c_no_own = {
	value = money_c_global_stokpile
	subtract = stockpiling_money_state
}

		add = market.mg:liberian_dollar_c.market_goods_buy_orders
	}
}
liberian_dollar_c_market_goods_sell_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:liberian_dollar_c.market_goods_sell_orders
	}
}
liberian_dollar_c_market_goods_delta = {
	value = liberian_dollar_c_market_goods_sell_orders
	subtract = liberian_dollar_c_market_goods_buy_orders
}
stockpiling_liberian_dollar_c_var_0 = {
	value = 0
	add = var:stockpiling_liberian_dollar_c_var_1
	add = var:circulating_liberian_dollar_c_var_1
}
stockpiling_liberian_dollar_state = {
	value = 0
	add  = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
				}
				add = var:stockpiling_liberian_dollar_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}
liberian_dollar_c_global_stokpile = {
	value = {
        add = {
            every_country = {
				add = stockpiling_liberian_dollar_state
            }
        }
	}
}

liberian_dollar_c_no_own = {
	value = liberian_dollar_c_global_stokpile
	subtract = stockpiling_liberian_dollar_state
}

tuareg_ouguiya_c_market_goods_buy_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:tuareg_ouguiya_c.market_goods_buy_orders
	}
}
tuareg_ouguiya_c_market_goods_sell_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:tuareg_ouguiya_c.market_goods_sell_orders
	}
}
tuareg_ouguiya_c_market_goods_delta = {
	value = tuareg_ouguiya_c_market_goods_sell_orders
	subtract = tuareg_ouguiya_c_market_goods_buy_orders
}
stockpiling_tuareg_ouguiya_c_var_0 = {
	value = 0
	add = var:stockpiling_tuareg_ouguiya_c_var_1
	add = var:circulating_tuareg_ouguiya_c_var_1
}
stockpiling_tuareg_ouguiya_state = {
	value = 0
	add  = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
				}
				add = var:stockpiling_tuareg_ouguiya_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}
tuareg_ouguiya_c_global_stokpile = {
	value = {
        add = {
            every_country = {
				add = stockpiling_tuareg_ouguiya_state
            }
        }
	}
}

tuareg_ouguiya_c_no_own = {
	value = tuareg_ouguiya_c_global_stokpile
	subtract = stockpiling_tuareg_ouguiya_state
}

        add = {
            every_country = {
				add = stockpiling_central_african_eco_state
            }
        }
	}
}

central_african_eco_c_no_own = {
	value = central_african_eco_c_global_stokpile
	subtract = stockpiling_central_african_eco_state
}

#east_african_eco
east_african_eco_c_market_goods_buy_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:east_african_eco_c.market_goods_buy_orders
	}
}
east_african_eco_c_market_goods_sell_orders = {
	value = {
		add = market.mg:east_african_eco_c.market_goods_sell_orders
	}
}
east_african_eco_c_market_goods_delta = {
	value = east_african_eco_c_market_goods_sell_orders
	subtract = east_african_eco_c_market_goods_buy_orders
}
stockpiling_east_african_eco_c_var_0 = {
	value = 0
	add = var:stockpiling_east_african_eco_c_var_1
	add = var:circulating_east_african_eco_c_var_1
}
stockpiling_east_african_eco_state = {
	value = 0
	add  = {
		every_scope_state = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
				}
				add = var:stockpiling_east_african_eco_state_1
			}
		}
	}
}
east_african_eco_c_global_stokpile = {
	value = {
        add = {
            every_country = {
				add = stockpiling_east_african_eco_state
            }
        }
	}
}

east_african_eco_c_no_own = {
	value = east_african_eco_c_global_stokpile
	subtract = stockpiling_east_african_eco_state
}

#money
buy_money_market_panel = {
	value = 1
	multiply = player.var:money_quantity
	multiply = {
		value = money_value_rapported_inflation
		divide = player.money_value_rapported_inflation
	}
}
sell_money_market_panel = {
	value = 1
	multiply = player.var:money_quantity
	multiply = {
		value = money_value_rapported_inflation
		divide = player.money_value_rapported_inflation
	}
}
sell_money_in_gold_market_panel = {
	value = player.var:money_quantity
	multiply = money_value_rapported_inflation
}

sell_limit_currency_var_0 = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_rank = rank_value:great_power
		}
		add = 100000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_rank = rank_value:major_power
		}
		add = 80000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_rank = rank_value:unrecognized_major_power
		}
		add = 60000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_rank = rank_value:unrecognized_regional_power
		}
		add = 4000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_rank = rank_value:minor_power
		}
		add = 20000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			country_rank = rank_value:unrecognized_power
		}
		add = 10000000
	}
}

sell_limit_currency_var_rest = {
	value = sell_limit_currency_var_0
	subtract = var:sell_limit_currency_var_1
}

gold_lent_to_other = { #buy
	value = 0

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			is_set = var:total_bond_value_10Y_1
			has_modifier = 10_year_buyer_maturity_buyer_1
		}
		add = var:total_bond_value_10Y_1
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			is_set = var:total_bond_value_10Y_2
			has_modifier = 10_year_buyer_maturity_buyer_2
		}

#money
stockpiling_money_state_buy_vriablity = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency < -3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -2
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_money_state_1_buy_in_gold_750000_scripted
		}
		add = 750000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -1
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_money_state_1_buy_in_gold_1250000_scripted
		}
		add = 1250000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 0
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_money_state_1_buy_in_gold_2500000_scripted
		}
		add = 2500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 1
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_money_state_1_buy_in_gold_5000000_scripted
		}
		add = 5000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 2
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_money_state_1_buy_in_gold_7500000_scripted
		}
		add = 7500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 3
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_money_state_1_buy_in_gold_10000000_scripted
		}
		add = 10000000
	}
}
stockpiling_money_state_sell_vriablity = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			stockpiling_money_state > 1
			stockpiling_money_state < 1000000
		}
		add = stockpiling_money_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 2
			stockpiling_money_state > 750000
		}
		add = 750000

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 1
			stockpiling_money_state > 1250000
		}
		add = 1250000

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 0
			stockpiling_money_state > 2500000
		}
		add = 2500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -1
			stockpiling_money_state > 5000000
		}
		add = 5000000 #{ 5000000 stockpiling_money_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -2
			stockpiling_money_state > 7500000
		}
		add = 7500000 #{ 7500000 stockpiling_money_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -3
			stockpiling_money_state > 10000000
		}
		add = 10000000 #{ 10000000 stockpiling_money_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency < -3
			stockpiling_money_state > 10000000
		}
		add = stockpiling_money_state
	}
}

	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency < -3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -2
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_1_buy_in_gold_750000_scripted
		}
		add = 750000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -1
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_1_buy_in_gold_1250000_scripted
		}
		add = 1250000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 0
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_1_buy_in_gold_2500000_scripted
		}
		add = 2500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 1
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_1_buy_in_gold_5000000_scripted
		}
		add = 5000000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 2
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_1_buy_in_gold_7500000_scripted
		}
		add = 7500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 3
			central_bank_gold_reserves_state > stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_1_buy_in_gold_10000000_scripted
		}
		add = 10000000
	}
}
stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state_sell_vriablity = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 1
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state < 1000000
		}
		add = stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 2
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 750000
		}
		add = 750000

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 1
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 1250000
		}
		add = 1250000

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 0
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 2500000
		}
		add = 2500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -1
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 5000000
		}
		add = 5000000 #{ 5000000 stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -2
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 7500000
		}
		add = 7500000 #{ 7500000 stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -3
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 10000000
		}
		add = 10000000 #{ 10000000 stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency < -3
			stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state > 10000000
		}
		add = stockpiling_egyptian_pound_state
	}
}

stockpiling_franc_state_sell_vriablity = {
	value = 0
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 3
		}
		add = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			stockpiling_franc_state > 1
			stockpiling_franc_state < 1000000
		}
		add = stockpiling_franc_state
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 2
			stockpiling_franc_state > 750000
		}
		add = 750000

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 1
			stockpiling_franc_state > 1250000
		}
		add = 1250000

	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = 0
			stockpiling_franc_state > 2500000
		}
		add = 2500000
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -1
			stockpiling_franc_state > 5000000
		}
		add = 5000000 #{ 5000000 stockpiling_franc_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -2
			stockpiling_franc_state > 7500000
		}
		add = 7500000 #{ 7500000 stockpiling_franc_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency = -3
			stockpiling_franc_state > 10000000
		}
		add = 10000000 #{ 10000000 stockpiling_franc_state }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			score_of_trust_with_reference_currency < -3
			stockpiling_franc_state > 10000000
		}
		add = stockpiling_franc_state
	}
}
